\documentclass{article}

\usepackage[margin=.7in]{geometry}
\usepackage{tikz}

\begin{document}

\tikzstyle{vertex} = [circle,draw,fill=white!20]

Configurations and bounds are given in the following table by $(g,x,y,z,w)$, where the polynomial Van der Waerden number
$PW(4, \{g\})$ is bounded above by $g(w)+1$ when $x,y,z,w$ form the following configuration:

\vspace{10pt}
\begin{center}
\begin{tikzpicture}
[scale=.4,auto=left]

\node [vertex, draw=red] (n1) at (1,7) {0};
\node [vertex, draw=blue] (n2) at (7,13) {$g(x)$};
\node [vertex, draw=green] (n3) at (7,1) {$g(y)$};
\node [vertex, draw=yellow] (n4) at (13,7) {$g(z)$};
\node [vertex, draw=red] (n5) at (21,7) {$w$};

\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n1) -- node {$g(x)$}(n2);
\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n1) -- node {$g(y)$}(n3);
\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n1) -- node [near start] {$g(z)$}(n4);
\draw (n2) -- node [pos=0.35] {$g(a)$}(n3);
\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n2) -- node {$g(b)$}(n4);
\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n2) -- node [near end]{$g(d)$}(n5);
\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n3) -- node {$g(c)$}(n4);
\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n3) -- node [near end]{$g(e)$}(n5);
\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n4) -- node {$g(f)$}(n5);

\end{tikzpicture}
\end{center}

As an example, where $g(x)=x^2$,

\vspace{10pt}
$ PW(4, x^2) < 1+290{,}085{,}289\times 290{,}085{,}289 = 84{,}149{,}474{,}894{,}213{,}522$
\vspace{10pt}

\begin{center}
\begin{tikzpicture}
[scale=.75,auto=left]

\node [vertex] (n1) at (1,7) {0};

\node [vertex] (n2) at (7,13) {112{,}529{,}664};

\node [vertex] (n3) at (7,1) {171{,}819{,}664};

\node [vertex] (n4) at (13,7) {260{,}273{,}689};

\node [vertex] (n5) at (21,7) {290{,}085{,}289};

\draw (n2) -- node [pos=0.35] {$7{,}700^2$}(n3);

\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n2) -- node {$12{,}155^2$}(n4);

\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n1) -- node {$10{,}608^2$}(n2);

\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n2) -- node [near end]{$13{,}325^2$}(n5);

\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n3) -- node {$9{,}405^2$}(n4);

\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n1) -- node {$13{,}108^2$}(n3);

\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n3) -- node [near end]{$10{,}875^2$}(n5);

\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n1) -- node [near start] {$16{,}133^2$}(n4);

\draw [{sloped,anchor=south,auto=false}] (n4) -- node {$5{,}460^2$}(n5);

\end{tikzpicture}
\vspace{10pt}

\end{center}
